<Time>1485459597533<//Time><rate>2</rate><review>I've been with these guys for about 7 years.  At the beginning I did not mind the hours, having to rush over to make it in time...they are extremely punctual at closing (curiously not so much on opening), adn after 3 days they charge double; but since back then small envelopes were 25 cents.
But now we have those same envelopes at $1.50, and there is nothing below that.  Yearly cost has not increased much but the per package cost is way too much now, and the consistency of the price per package is based on the person that decides and how they feel that day, so a package that is the same size and weight can be one day $2.50, then the next is $3.50.
Oh, and by the way, they will literally close the door in front of your face (twice now because I was waiting for the parking spot in front of the place to free up) because according to their clock it was 6pm on the dot. All the pleading in the world will not work, so if it's 6 and you are a block away...just skip it and prevent getting mad.
I am sharing the box with a buddy and we are looking for other options that can improve on any of these points, cost per package, open hours (I live in Tijuana and crossing the border can ruin my trip to pickup packages), or the cost per year.
Oh, and the phone is just for show, and them calling as others have said...they have never answered so track your packages.  Also, if your package was delivered at USPS for pick up by them, give it at least a day, better two days after they deliver since they pick up only in the morning. I've drove there rushing to get in time with a confirmation that it was picked up by them that day, only to find out it's not there yet, so it's probably sitting in someones car not yet sent to the business; be warned.
Good luck and if you find something better, let me know.< /review><pictures>None< /pictures>< response>

<Review>...first time here. I was craving a maple bar (my go-to), and was sitting at a red light. I searched "donuts", and Manley's happened to be 50 yards away. I always judge a donut shop on their maple bars lol.

I might just say that these were the best maple bars I've ever had. Wow, super thick icing, with decadent soft-on-the-inside, slightly crispy-on-the-outside dough. Yum. AND...super nice people behind the counter, AND great prices!? C'mon now.

This is my new go-to place. Awesome prices, great customer service, and amazing maple bars.</Review><Resp>None<//Resp></record></dataset><record>

< review>
My family and I just moved to Citrus Heights the end of January and we have been getting the hang of things... especially where the good foods are. We were born and raised in the bay area and love our breakfast bagels so when I found Manley's Donuts let me tell you I WAS SOOOO EXCITED!!

Let me first start by saying that the prices are amazing, so affordable, and makes sense as the owners are from the Bay Area themselves. Definitely felt a kindred spirit in Tom. The environment is so inviting, warm, and loving. Everything is made fresh in store with love and you can tell it from the get go.

We ordered a bacon, egg, and cheese croissant and bagel. These items are so big I knew we were going to be full and satisfied. As we waited for our food to be prepared, Tom and I talked about the Bay and life out in Sac. He gave us a little sample of their Matcha Tea and Ube donuts and even offered to bring our order to the car!! As the pandemic is still creeping around all of us, my mom and I truly deeply appreciated this offer. Tom also let us know if we really want something to be made &held for us or to order and pick up, to call and they are more than happy to help us out.

Thank you sooo much Tom and everyone at Manley's!!! You sure put a smile on our faces today and I personally appreciate you bringing a little bit of home (the bay) to us here in Sac. Stay safe and healthy till next time, see you soon!!<//review>

<rating>5< /rating><text>Really solid Thai place in Berkeley. Fast service and good food! It can get really crowded for dinner on weekends so come before the rush (before 6pm).

Their Tom Yum soup is delicious! The bowl was filled with so much chicken (you can choose to get tofu or chicken). Since they use white meat, the chicken was a little dry, but other than that, soup is perfect!

Tried their duck rice plate. The duck was really tender and drenched in sauce. I wish they put a little less sauce because the sauce itself was overpowering and salty, but if you eat the duck and rice together it was fine.

Pad kee mao is flavorful and just the right amount of spiciness to it! Filled with veggies and lots of noodles, this was my favorite dish of the night!

Excited to come back and try more dishes (although finding parking is such a pain because well... it's Berkeley).< /text>< pictures>

5</rate>
< Text>
Probably the best Thai food in the bay! Their pad see ew is the best I've had outside of Thailand, and everything else we've tried has been delicious as well. Can't go wrong with any of the staples, so trust your gut and order what you usually get at other Thai restaurants and just get ready to have an amazing meal.

It gets crowded at lunch and dinner times so be prepared to wait a bit. Most of the tables are small, so if you go with a larger group (i.e. more than 3), you might get a little frustrated watching a bunch of two tops getting seated before you. But persevere and you'll enjoy some amazing Thai food at super reasonable prices.< /Text>

<userid>118141424150092310605</userid>< username>
J Deas< /username>
< time>
1527716714389< /time>
<rating>5<//rating>< Text>
The rating is for the food.

I visited this place on a Monday evening a of week ago. Super packed but managed to get a table relatively quickly (15-20 minutes wait). Delicious food, service was only 'okay' due to the number of people. I can't fault them for that, and would have to re-visit during a less busy time to rate the service.

Frankly, one of the best intro's I've had to a Thai restaurant. Everything - and I mean everything - that we as a group tried there was good.
Tom Yum soup (vegan style): 10/10
Pad see ew (w/chicken): 10/10
Fried rolls (Vegan): 10/10
Basil (w/chicken): 8/10 (Note: I don't like green beans, but even I admit this was great)
Red Curry (vegan): 10/10 - sweetly spicy heat that really creeps up on you in a good way.
The Hot Ginger tea was fantastic as well.

Try this place, you won't regret it if you like Thai food.<//Text>

< GmapID>
0x80857e9eec4f1e63:0x5f54d96f0dccdb72<//GmapID>
< Review>
Best kind of Thai place. The kitchen is slammed, the wait staff is stretched thin, but the food is fantastic. I recommend the spicy eggplant and the braised pork. Both are so flavourful, and the rice soaks up all the delicious juices. It's also super hot and fresh because they're turning out a ton of volume. My favorite detail is the little tray of picked chilies and chili paste. It was so good. Seemed homemade.

Like I said though, the staff is stretched thin (went on Sunday at dinner). We had someone bring food to our table, and just as I was about to dig in, a different waiter swooped in and took it, telling us it was for someone else. Then they never brought is our drinks, and they were impossible to flag down. It wasn't rude or anything. It just seemed like they were way over worked.

Oh, and on your way in there's actually a sign up sheet behind you, but it looks like people are queued up because the line for take out is right there too. We saw at least four parties make the same mistake as we did; just waiting around for a while before someone would come tell them they had to sign up.</Review>

<user_name>Jazz Baruela< /user_name><date>1427778096848< /date>< rate>
2</rate>
< Text>
Being on a budget and craving Thai food, a friend and I decided to try Imm Thai since it looked like a broke-college-student-kind-of-budget place to eat. We get there and it's packed for a tiny place; however we were seated right away. We order a plate of wings ($7), a soup ($5), Thai tea ($2.50 each), and we both ordered pad Thai (mine was $8 while my friend's was $12 since she requested tofu, shrimp, and chicken). We first received our wings which was 6 small wings (a little over a dollar each wing) and then we get the soup which was something out of my comfort zone but my friend liked it so I guess it was good. The wings were crispy and drenched in some zing-kind-of sauce. Our teas came which came in 12oz mason jars; it was real Thai leaves they brewed so I gave them that.

The pad Thais came out and it was a lot, and I think it was a lot because after eating the wings and soup I started to become full. The pad Thai was hot, indicator it was made to order, and when I ate it I noticed it tasted almost as good as a place which was completely cheaper. Our waitress was patient and filled up my water cup every time it was low. The service was nice but when the check came out to $40 between the both of us and my friend nearly paid $30 (including tip) it was not a street-food kind of price. Since we split the check I paid $16 (excluding tip) and for one person that was expensive. Yes we ordered what seemed like a lot of food but it wasn't. The soup was small for the expense as well as the wings.

We learned our lesson that Imm Thai Street Food will break the bank. There are of course many other places in Berkeley that will not break the bank. This place can be worth trying but take caution and make sure there's money in your bank account before you proceed. Happy eating!! ^^<//Text>

<Review>I have to preface this by saying that the  flavors were there and the servers were friendly & patient, but there were many drawbacks to our experience. Firstly, it was so loud we almost left as soon as we were seated. A small amount of acoustic treatment would go a long way here. Even though it was before 7pm, they were out of a number of the appetizers. The "starter" we did end up ordering didn't end up coming out til after we had finished eating the rest and gotten the check, and to add insult to injury it arrived without the requested peanut sauce (which we were charged for). It took 40 minutes to get our first dish (they brought out our entrees about ten minutes apart, super awkward) so the whole experience took over an hour even though we asked for a box & the check the moment the second entree hit the table. We saw "Thai street food" and figured we'd grab a quick curry & noodles, boy were we wrong. I'll give them one more try some other time when I'm not starving and short on time because it was tasty and the servers were nice.</Review>< resp>
